frere hugo de loubeux verdala dei gratia sacra domu hospitali sancti
ioanni hierosolymitani magist humili pauperumqu iesu christi custo
vniuersi et singuli principibu ecclesiastici et secularibu
archiepiscopi episcopi ducibu marchionibu baronibu nobilibu
capitanei vicedomini praefecti castellani admiralij et
quibuscunqu triremium vel aliorum nauigiorum patroni ac ciuitatum
rectoribu potestatibu ac magistratibu caeterisqu officialibu et
quibuscunqu personi cuiusui dignitati gradu statu et conditioni
fuerint vbilibet locorum et terrarum constituti salutem

notum facimu et verbo veritati attestamur come nel mese di maggio
prossim passato le nostr galer vennero dal viaggio di barberia doue
hauendo mandato per socorrer vn galionetto de christiani che hauea dato
trauerso quell parti essendo arriuati sopra questa isola alla part de
ponent trouarono vno naue inglesa sopra cargo de essa il magnifico
giouanni keal et dauid filli patrono volendo la reconoscer che naue
foss han visto che se metteua ordin per defendersi dubitando che
dett nostr galer fossero de inimici et per che vn marinaro riuoltos
contra la volonta de detti magnifico giouanni keal et dauid filli habbi
tirato vn tiro di artiglieria verso vna de dett galer et che non se
amangnaua la vela de la maiestra secondo la volonta de detti magnifico
giouanni keal et dauid filli patrono furimensata detta naue nel present
gener porto di malta secondo lordin del venerando general de dett
galer et essendo qua monsignor inquisitor ha impedita quella per conto
del sancto officio et si died part alla santita di nostro signor
gregorio papa xiij A la fin fu licenciata per andarsen al suo viaggio
han donqu humilment supplicato detti magnifico giouanni keal et dauid
filli per nome et part delli magnifici edwardo osborn senator et richardo
staper merchanti inglesi della nobil citta di londra et anco di tomaso
wilkinson scriuano piloti nocheri et marinari gli volessimo dare le
nostr letter patent et saluo condutto accioch potranno andar et
ritornar quando gli parera commodo con alcuna roba et mercantia loro
benuista si come noi essendo cosa giusta et che retornera commoda
nostra relligion et questi forrestieri per tenor de li presenti se gli
habiamo concess con le condition pero infra scritt videlicet

che ogni volta che detti mercadanti con sopradetta naue con altra non
porterano mercanti de contrabando et che constara per fede authentica et
con letter patent de sanita poteran liberalment victualiars de tutt
le victuari necessari et praticar questa isola et dominij et poi
partisen et seguir suo viaggio per doue volessero leuant altrou
come tutti altri vaselli et specialment de francesi et aitri nationi et
die venderi et comprar qual si voglia mercantia loro benuista

item che potera portar poluer de canon et di archibuso salnitro
carboni di petra rosetta platin de rame stagno accial ferro carise
commun tela grossa bianca per far tend de galer ball de ferro de
calibro petr de molino fine arbor et antenn de galer bastardi et
alteri Et conclusion hauenda visto che loro per il tempo che
restarano qua si portorno da fide et catholici christiani et che sua
sanctita habbia trouata bono il saluo condutto del gran turko loro
concesso per il timor della armata turkesca et di altri vaselli de
inimici inherendo alla volonta di sua sanctita et massim per che hauera
de andar et passar per diuersi lochi et tanto lontani come ingilterra
flandra et tutti patri di ponent et altrou noi ha parso farl le
present nostr letter patent com fidel conuersator nostro accio piu
securament et sensa obstaculo possa andar et ritornar quando li parera
con detta naue con altr loro benuista per tanto donqu tutti et
ciascun di voi sudetti affectuosament pregamo che per qual si voglia de
vostra iurisdition alla qual detto magnifico giouanni keal et dauid
filli anom quo supra con la naue et marinari de detti loro principali
altri caschera nauigar passar et venir sicurament alla libera
sensa alcuno disturbo altro impedimento li lasciat et facciat
lasciar stare et passar tornar et quando li parera partir talment
che per amor et contemplation nostra il detto magnifico giouanni keal
nome quo supra con le naue marinari et mercantia non habbi difficulta
fastidio et ritention alcuna anzi se gli dia ogni agiuto et fauor cosa
degnadi voi giusta et noi gratissima de recompensaruila con vagul et
maggior seruitio quando dalloccasion ne saremo rechiesti Et finalment
commandammo tutti et qual si voglia relligiosi et frati de nostra
relligion di qual si voglia condition grado et stato che siano et
tutti riceuitori et procuratori nostri tutti et qual si voglia priorati
nostri deputati et deputandi vertu di santa obedientia et attuti nostri
vassal et alla giurisdition di nostri relligion sogetti che tale et
per tale tenghino et reputino il detto magnifico giouanni keal nome vt
supra naue marinari et mercantia sensa permitter che nel detto suo
viaggio alcun altro iuogo sia molestato qual si voglia manera
impedito anzi rutt le cose sue et negotij loro sian da voi agioutati et
continuament fauoriti In cuiu rei testimonium bulla nostra magistrali
cera nigra praesentibu est impressa data melita conuentu nostro die
duodecimo mensi iulij

A command chio

vobi beg et cadi et ermini qui esti chio significamu quod
serenissima regina maiestati anglia orat qui est excelsa porta per
litera significauit nobi quod ex nauibu anglici vna naui venisset ad
portum chico et illinc constantinopolim recto cursu voluisset venir et
contra priuilegium detenuisti et non siuisti venir haec praedictu
orat significauit nobi et petiuit nobi hoc negocio hoc mandatum
vt naue anglica veniant et rediant nostra dition caesarea
priuilegium datum et concessum est ex part serenitati caesarea nostra et
huiu priuilegij copia data est sub insigni nostro Et contra nostrum
priuilegium caesareum quod ita agitur quae est causa quando cum hoc mandato
nostro homin illorum ad vo venerint ex praedicta anglia si naui venerit
ad portum vestrum et si re et merc ex naue exemerint et vendiderint
et tricessimam secundam partem reddiderint et re quae manserint
constantinopolim auferr velint patiantur Et si aliqui contra
priuilegium et articulo eiu aliquid ageret non sinati nec vo facit
et impediri non sinati eo vt recta constantinopolim venient sui
negotiationibu sine molestia ess possint Et quicunqu contra hoc
mandatum et priuilegium nostrum aliquid fecerit nobi signif huic
mandato nostro et insigni fidem adhibet In principio mensi decembri

Of citi alexandria

alexandria ancient citi africa situat seasid
containeth seuen mile circuit enuiron two wall one
neer high tower wall within farr higher
without great ditch round yet
citi strong reason great antiquiti almost
half destroy ruinat the greatness citi
doubl habit compass doubl wall
might trueli said two alexandria one build vpon
anoth vnder foundat said citi great
habit incred huge piller true part
vnderneath remaineth day inhabit corrupt air
also time consumeth thing great
ruinat It might well sayd founder hereof worthi
enterpris likewis build hereof work
worthi himself name own name thi citi hath one
defect subiect euill ayr one proceedeth
hollowness vnderneath issueth infinit moistur
true ayr without doth evid testifi
subtil holesom beneath the water hereof salt
reason soil self likewis and therefor
inhabit time riuer nilu floweth accustom
open great ditch head wherof extendeth said riuer
thenc conueigh within half mile alexandria
consequ mean conductpip water commeth vnto
cestern alexandria full seru citi one
inund anoth within citi pyramid mention
histori great import without citi La colonna di
pompeio pillar pompey height thickness
suppos like whole world besid within
citi noth import saue litl castl guard
ianizari alexandria hath three port one toward rossetto
anoth land ward third sea ward call
babelbar without appeareth broad iland call ghesira
moor tongu wholi iland litl point corner
thereof toucheth firm land therefor may call peninsula
say almost iland hereupon build mani hous

vnfitli giuen vnto men iudgement time past
hath been water midst port

constantinopl ornament mesquita turkish templ

Of mighti citi cairo

cairo containeth circuit eighteen mile inhabit

haue begunn build new hous without citi

Of patriark greec

In cairo two patriark one greek anoth
iacobit the greek patriark call gioechni age one
hundr thirteen yeer good holi man they say
soldan gauri egypt reign done miracl follow
good patriark enui iew countrey none
caus good work holi life happen say
disput certain hebrew presenc
sultan reason law faith sayd vnto one
miscreant sith thou beleeuest faith christ take
drink potion giue thee thi christ true
messia true god sayd deliuer thee daunger To
auncient patriark answer content whereupon curs
iew brought cupp venem deadli poyson could
found holi patriark hau perceiu said In name
father sonn holi ghost hau sayd
drank quit vp done took dropp pure water put
cup gaue vnto iew say vnto
name christ haue drunk thi poyson therefor name thi
expect messia drink water mine within thine own cupp
whereupon iew took cup hand patriark
hau drunk water within half hour burst sunder and
patriark none hurt saue becam somewhat pale sight
remain euer and miracl meriteth call
less done great commend holi patriark
presenc thousand person name soldan egypt
see despight iew vnto own cost confus
compel make conduct mani engin commeth
castl nilu abou mention and triumphant patriark
long sinc aliu perfect health god continu long time


Of prepar carouan goe mecca

As touch carouan goeth mecca vnderstood
mahometan obseru kind lent continu one whole moon
moueabl ceremoni sometim falleth high sometim low
yeer call tongu ramazan feast call bairam
dure time lent intend goe vnto mecca resort
vnto cairo twenti day feast carouan
readi depart voyag thither resort great multitud
peopl asia grecia barbaria goe voyag moou
deuotion traffiqu sake pass away time
now within few day feast goe voyag depart
citi two leagu vnto place call birca expect
captain carouan thi place hath great pond caus
inund nilu made camel beast may
drink therein whereof name mule camel dromedari
least forti thousand person follow carouan
eueri yeer fifti thousand few less accord
time moreouer eueri three yeer renu captain
carouan call arabian tongu amarilla haggi captain
pilgrim grand signior giueth eueri voyag eighteen
purs conteyn six hundr twenti fiue ducat
gold behoof carouan also doe alm
vnto needful pilgrim thi captain besid seruingmen
follow hath also four chausi seru likewis hath
securiti carouan four hundr souldier wit two
hundr spachi horsemen mount dromedari two hundr
ianizari ride vpon camel the chausi spachi charg
captain ianizari prouision made
cairo the spachi wear cap bonnet like cap
sergeant ianizari anoth sort lapp fall
down behind like frenchhood hau great piec
wrought siluer head the charg caus carouan
march good array need requireth
commaund captain carouan moreouer
captain hath guid eight pilot offic alway
stabl firm heir heir goe guid
carouan shew way well experienc place
night gouern marin starr sidenot
piec dri wood stead torch these also vse send
four fiue men cari piec dri wood giue light
goe way time ill hap
wander astray way cast down beaten
mani bastonado vpon sole feet seru
perpetual remembr the captain carouan hath lieuten
accompani continu fifteen spachi hath charg set
carouan order caus depart iourney
need requireth voyag offic while goe
foreward sometim come behind rereward
sometim march one side sometim spi
coast clear the carouan carrieth six piec
ordin drawen camel seru terrifi arabian
also make triumph mecca place the marchant
follow carouan carri marchandis cloth silk
coral tinn other wheat rise sort grain some sell
way mecca eueri one bringeth someth gain
marchandis goeth land payeth custom
goeth sea bound pay tenn hundr


the begin voyag

the feast carouan setteth forth captain
retinu offic resort vnto castl cairo basha
giueth vnto eueri man garment captain wrought
gold other seru accord degre moreouer
deliuereth vnto chisua talnabi signifieth arabian
tongu the garment prophet vestur silk wrought
midst letter gold signifi La illa illalla mahumet
resullala say there god god ambassadour
mahumet thi garment made purpos couer top botom
litl hous mecca stand midst mesquita hous
say build abraham sonn ismael after
deliuereth gate made purpos foresaid hous abraham
wrought fine gold excel workmanship
thing great valu besid deliuereth vnto couer
green veluet made maner pyrami nine palm high
artifici wrought fine gold couer tomb
prophet within medina tomb built manner
pyrami besid couer brought mani other gold
silk ornament sayd tomb which thing
consign basha departeth place captain

what time carouan trauelleth resteth

It note cairo mecca make day iourney
thereabout great day iournei for custom
carouan trauell much rest littl ordinarili iourney
maner they trauell two clock morn vntill sunn
rise hau rest till noon set forward continu
till night also rest again abouesaid till two
clock order obseru vntill end voiag neuer
chang except place whereof hereaft speak
respect water rest sometim day half
obseru refresh themselu otherwis man beast would die


In order carouan trauelleth

the maner order carouan obserueth march It
goeth diuid three part wit foreward main battel
rereward In foreward go pilot chau
hath four knaue ech knaue carrieth sinew bul
end occas requireth bastonado may giuen
deseru these knaue cast offendour down turn vp sole
feet made fast staff giu perpetual remembr
behold thi chau captain foreward
commandeth light carri trauell
night also go foreward santon red turbant vpon
head eat ride cost captain
carouan these santon carouan arriueth good lodg
suddenli haue escri place cri horribl voyc
say good chear good chear neer wish lodg for
good new chief compani bestow beneuol vpon
In foreward goeth neer third part peopl
carouan behind go alway spachi arm sword bow
arrow defend thieue next vnto foreward within
quarter mile followeth main battel
drawen sayd six piec ordin gunner fifteen
spachi archer and next vnto commeth chief physicion
old man authoriti hau mani medicin oyntment salu
like refresh sick hau also camel
sick ride haue hors beast next vnto goeth
one camel alon fairest found great industri
sought greatest fairest may found within dominion
grand signior thi camel also deck cloth gold
silk carieth littl chest made pure legmam made likeness
ark old testament abouesayd made pure legmam
without gold thing cost within chest alcoran
written great letter gold bound between two tabl
massi gold chest voyag couer silk
entr mecca couer cloth gold adorn
iewel like enter medina the camel
aforesayd carrieth chest compass mani arabian
singer musician alway sing play vpon instrument after
folow fiften fair camel eueri one cari one
abouesayd vestur couer topp toe silk behind
goe twenti camel carri money apparel
prouision amir el cheggi captain carouan after foloweth
royal standard grand signior accompani continu
musician captain fiue twenti spachi archer
chau marueil thing goe peopl
camel follow carouan behind less mile foloweth
rereward whereof greater part pilgrim occas whereof
merchant seek alway foreward
securiti good pilgrim haue litl loos care
though come behind behind alway goe fiue twenti
spachi well arm anoth chau captain forti
arabian archer guard rereward and carouan
goeth alway along red sea bank go forth haue
right hand therfor two hundr ianissari part three
compani goe vpon left hand well arm mount vpon camel bound
one anoth vpon side danger thieue
danger captain carouan alway go
peopl sometim one side sometim neuer
keep firm place continu accompani chau
spachi arm mount vpon dromedari  musician viol
hand ceas sound till captain take rest
vpon attend till time entreth pauillion

Of thing notabl seen voyag way

becaus way mani thing found woorthi memori
carouan seldom resteth place habit
way few yea rather carouan resteth altogeth
field therefor voyag wee one make mention certain
castl found way bee name agerut nachel acba
biritem muel ezlem Of fiue two first kept moor
three turk guard haue eight men tenn
eueri castl four fiue smerigli seru
keep water arabian carouan com thither may
haue wherewithal refresh self agerut distant suez port
red sea eight mile alway resid fiue twenti
galli grand signior keep sea nachel distant
sea day iourney the wall acba found vpon red
sea bank biritem muel likewis dash waue sea
ezlem distant thenc abou day iourney these fiue castl
abouesayd forc altogeth defend themselu agaynst
hundr men the carouan depart birca vntill agerut findeth
water way drink neither agerut till nachel
nachel till acba between acba biritem found two water one
call agiam el cassap magarraxiaibi say
riuer iethro father law mose place
mention second chapter exodu whither sayd mose
fledd anger pharao would haue kill hee
slain aegyptian fought hebrew place stood

true musulmani commaund done

Of serifo king mecca

the serifo descend prophet mahomet fatma daughter
good prophet alli husband sonn law mahumet
issu male saue stock serifo eldest sonn
whereof realm commeth success thi realm hath reuenu
royal eueri yeer half million gold litl
prophet kinr descend blood almost
innumer call emyri say lord these goe
cloth green least haue turbant green bee knowen
neither permit christian
dwell traffiqu countrey goe cloth green neither may
haue thing green say lawful
misbeleeu wear colour wherein great friend prophet
god mahomet woont apparel


Of citi mecca

the citi mecca arabian tongu call macca say
habit thi citi inuiron exceed high barren
mountain plain between sayd mountain citi
mani pleasant garden groweth great abundaunc figg
grape appl melon there also great abund good water
flesh bread thi citi hath wall
containeth circuit fiue mile the hous handsom
commodi built like hous itali the palac
serifo sumptuou gorgeous adorn the women place
courteou iocund loueli fair allur eye hote
libidin naughti pack the men place
giuen abhomin curs opprobri vice whereof men
women make small account reason pond zun zun wherein
hau wash themselu opinion although like dog
return vomit yet clens sinn whatsoeuer
sin hereaft larg discours In midst
citi great mosquita hous abraham stand
middest thereof mosquita built time prophet
liu It four squar great containeth two mile
circuit say half mile side also made maner
cloister midst thereof separ rest
abouesayd hous abraham also galleri round maner
street partit diuid one street
pillar whereof marbl other lime stone thi
famou sumptuou mosquita hath  gate  steepl whenc
talismani call peopl mosquita and pilgrim
prouid tent resort hither deuotion men
women lie togeth aloft beneath one vpon anoth hous
praier becommeth wors sometim den thieue


Of hous abraham

the hous abraham also four squar made speckl stone
pace high circuit and vpon one side hous within
wall stone span long half span broad stone
say hous build fell down heauen
fall whereof heard voyc wheresoeu stone fell
built hous god wherein god hear sinner moreouer
say stone fell heauen black
white whitest snow reason hath bene oft kiss
sinner therewith becom black pilgrim bound
kiss stone otherwis cari sinn home
the entranc hous small made maner window
high ground man reach pain enter
thi hous hath without  pillar brass set vpon cubik squar
stone red green pillar sustain ought el saue
threed copper reacheth one anoth whereunto
fasten mani burn lamp these pillar brass caus
made sultan soliman grandfath sultan amurath emperor after
hau entr difficulti abouesayd stand
entranc two pillar marbl wit side one In midst
three aloeswood thick couer tile
india  colour seru vnderpropp terratza It
dark hardli see within want light without
euill smell without gate fiue pase abouesayd pond zun zun
bless pond angel lord shew vnto agar
while went seek water sonn ismael drink


Of ceremoni pilgrim

In begin haue sayd mahumetan haue two feast
yeer the one call pascha di ramazaco say the feast
fast feast fast holden thirti day feast
wherein carouan trauelleth mecca the call feast
ramm wherin abiliti bound sacrific
ramm call bine bairam say the great feast and
carouan departeth cairo thirti day littl feast
likewis come hither fiue six day great feast
end pilgrim may haue time feast finish rite
ceremoni depart carouan
guid experienc way goe vnto citi
twenti thirti compani think good walk
street ascendeth litl litl till come vnto certain
gate whereupon written side marbl stone babel salema
arabian tongu signifieth gate health and
place descri great mosquita enuironeth hous
abraham descri reuerent salut twise say salem
alech iara sul alia say peac thee ambassadour god
thi salut end proceed way find arch
vpon right hand whereon ascend fiue step vpon
great voyd place made stone descend fiue step
proceed space flightshoot find anoth arch like vnto
first way one arch go come
time say alwai prayer say afflict
agar sayd while sought found water sonn ismael
drink thi ceremoni end pilgrim enter mosquita
draw neer vnto hous abraham goe round
seuen time alway say thi hous god seruant
abraham thi done goe kiss black stone abouesayd after
go vnto pond zun zun apparel wash
themselu head foot say tobah allah tobah allah
say pardon lord pardon lord drink also waier
mudi filthi ill sauour wise wash water
eueri one returneth place abod ceremoni eueri one
bound doe least but haue mind ouergo
fellow goe paradis rest doe
day carouan remaineth


what carouan doeth hau rest mecca

captain compani setteth forward toward mountain
pardon call arabian tongu iabel arafata thi
mountain distant mecca  mile mid way thereto
place call mina say the hauen litl thenc
great pillar hereaft speak now first touch
mountain pardon rather call litl hill
mountain low litl delight pleasant contain
circuit two mile enuiron round goodliest plain
euer man eie could seen plain likewis compass
exceed high mountain sort one goodliest
situat world seemeth verili natur hath therein
shew cun make place vnder mountain pardon
broad pleasant vpon side toward mecca mani pipe
water clear fair fresh abou wholesom fall

Of three carouan

the day carouan cairo commeth place hither come
carouan also one damasco arabia like maner
inhabit ten day iourney round one time
seen abou  person  cattel
now compani meet togeth place night
feast three host cast themselu triangl set
mountain midst night noth
heard seen gunshot firework sundri sort

wonderful after day feast come
rest silenc day attend thing
sacrific oblat prayer vnto god euen
haue hors mount thereon approch nigh vnto mountain
haue hors make best shift foot
giu euer vnto captain cairo chief place second
captain damasco third captain arabia
approch abouesayd commeth squar squir one
santon mount camel well furnish side
mountain ascendeth fiue step pulpit made purpos
silent turn face toward peopl maketh short sermon
tenour folow

the summ santon sermon

the summ doubl doctor sermon thu much brief He sheweth
mani great benefit god hath giuen mahumetan peopl
hand belou friend prophet mahomet hau deliuer
seruitud sinn idolatri time
drown gaue vnto hous abraham wherein
heard likewis mountain pardon mean
whereof might obtain grace remiss sinn ad
merciful god liberal giuer good thing
commaund secretari abraham build hous mecca
successour might make prayer vnto bee heard time
mountain world came togeth thither sufficienci
stone build hereof except litl low hill
pouerti could go discharg debt becam
sorrow weep beyond measur space thirti yeer
end whereof eternal god hau piti compass vpon
poor mountain said vnto weep daughter thi bitter
plaint haue ascend vp mine ear therefor comfort thi self
caus shall goe visit hous friend
abraham shall absolu sinn vnless
first come doe thee reuerenc keep place holiest
feast and haue command vnto peopl mouth friend
prophet mahumet thi said exhorteth vnto loue god

signior host third peopl prayer
one voic cri say amni Ia alla amni Ia alla say
Be lord lord thu hau santon bless

whereof wee haue made mention In return end plain
abouesaid  piller wit two ech side way
midst whereof say needful eueri one pass say
passeth without looseth merit pilgrimag
gotten also mountain pardon vntill pass
said piller none dare look backward fear least sinn
hath left mountain return again be past piller
eueryon lighteth down seek sandi field   litl
stone gather bound hankerchiff carri
abouesaid place mina stay  day time
fair free frank al custom and place
piller togeth set diuer place prophet
saith three apparit diuel made vnto abraham
ismael sonn amongst make mention isaac
neuer bene born So say bless god hau command
abraham faithful seruant sacrific first begotten ismael
old abraham went accord god wil met infernal
enemi shape man demand whither went
answer went sacrific sonn ismael god command
against diuel exclaim said Oh dote old man sith god
thine old age hath marueil giuen thee son nation
shalb bless wherefor giu credit vnto vain dream wilt thou kill
much thou hast desir intir lou but abraham
shake proceed way whereupon diuel see word
could preuail father attempt sonn say ismael
haue regard vnto thyself betim thing danger
wherefor answer child becaus saith diuel thi dote father
seeketh take away thi life for occas said ismael becaus
saith enemi saith god hath command which ismael
hear hee took vp stone threw say auzu billahi minal
scia itanil ragini say defend god diuel
offend would say wee ought obey command god
resist diuel al forc but return purpos
pilgrim abod goe visit three piller
throw away littl stone gather while
repeat word say ismael said diuell
withstood from henc half mile mountain whither abraham
went sacrific sonn abouesaid In mountain great
den whither pilgrim resort make prayer great
stone natur separ midst say ismael

prooue would cut make triall diuid stone two

Of grida

grida port neer mecca therefor wee say mecca grida
make two small day iourney place ill
traueil daytim reason great heat sunn
therefor depart euen mecca morn
sunneris arriu half way certain habit
well furnish good inn lodg especi women ynough
voluntarili bestow alm vpon poor pilgrim likewis
depart next euen morn come vnto grida thi
citi found vpon red sea bank enuiron wal tower
landward continu time almost consum wast
side seaward stand vnwall grida hath three gate one
ech side third midst toward land call
port mecca neer vnto  turk vpon old tower
guard thereof four faulcon vpon one corner citi
landward also seaward wall ioyneth water
late made fort like vnto bulwark haue plant
piec best ordin might well kept
guard more outward toward sea vpon farthest old tower
fiue good piec men guard sidenot the portug
greatli fear red sea On side citi end
wall late build bulwark strong well guard
saniaccho turk wel prouid ordin
necessari munit fortifi none
caus fear suspit portug and port
good vain port wors danger
full rock sand wise ship come
neer perforc ride least two mile sidenot forti
fifti rich ship arriu yeer grida At port arriu eueri yeer
forti fifti great shipp laden spice rich marchand
yeeld custom ducat half whereof goeth vnto
grand signior half serifo and none
thing worthi mention grida wil return carouan
hath almost rest enough


Of go medina

the carouan departeth medina return way came vnto
bedrihonem abouesayd leaue ordin cariag
whereof haue need pilgrim haue seen medina
aforetim desir see again stay place
expect carouan rest vntill carouan go bedrihonem
medina alway find goodli habit abund
sweet water date enough within foureteen mile medina

Of medina

medina littl citi great antiqu contain circuit abou
two mile hau therein one castl old weak guard
aga fifti piec artilleri good the hous
thereof fair well situat built lime stone
midst citi stand fouresquar mosquita great
mecca goodli rich sumptuou build within
corner thereof tomb built vpon four piller vault
vnder pauement bindeth four piller togeth the
tomb high farr exceedeth heighth mosquita
couer lead top inamel gold half
moon vpon top within pauement artifici
wrought gold below round great stair yron
ascend vp vntill midst piller midst thereof
buri bodi mahomet chest yron cleau
adam mani affirm know trueth thereof moreouer ouer
bodi haue built tomb speckl stone brace half
high margin note Or fathom ouer anoth legmam
fouresquar maner pyrami after round sepultur
hangeth curtain silk letteth sight without
see sepultur beyond mosquita
two sepulchr couer green cloth one
buri fatma daughter mahomet alli buri
husband sayd fatma the attend vpon sepulchr
fifti eunuch white tawni neither grant
enter within tomb sau three white eunuch oldest best
credit vnto lawful enter twise day light
lamp doe seruic all eunuch attend without
seruic mosquita two sepulchr fatma
alli eueri one may go touch pleasur take
earth deuotion mani


Of thing without citi

without citi eueri side fair garden mani
fountain sweet water infinit pond abund fruit
much honest liu place pleasant delightful
thi citi hath three gate one hospital caus built
cassachi call rosel wife sultan solimam grandfath
emperour the sayd hospital hath nought el woorthi mention saue
fair built hath larg reuenu belong thereunto
nourisheth mani poor peopl A mile citi certain hous
whereof affirm one mahumet lifetim
dwelt thi hous hath eueri side mani fair date tree amongst
two grow one stock exceed high
say prophet graf own hand fruit thereof
alway sent constantinopl present vnto grand signior
sayd bless fruit prophet nere vnto date tree
fair fountain cleer sweet water conduct pipe
brought citi medina also littl mosquita
wherein three place count holi greatli reuerenc first
affirm prophet made first prayer knew
god second whither went would see holi hous
abraham sate intent say mountain
open topp bottom shew hous close again
third holi place midst sayd mosquita
tomb made lime stone fouresquar full sand wherein
say buri bless camel mahumet alway woont
ride vpon On side citi tomb holi
mahumetan eueri one hath tomb built vpon four piller
amongst three companion mahumet wit abubacar
ottoman omar visit pilgrim holi place


the offer vestur vnto sepulchr

the carouan come medina two hour day rest
till euen captain compani pilgrim
setteth forward greatest pomp possibl take
vestur made maner pyrami mani gold
silk departeth go thorow midst citi vntill come
mosquita hau prai presenteth vnto tomb prophet
eunuch receiu hand readi vestur sayd
tomb certain eunuch entr take away old vestur lay
new burn old one diuid gold thereof
equal portion after present vestur ornament
mosquita also peopl without deliuer vnto eunuch ech man
somewhat touch tomb therewith keep reliqu
great deuotion thi ceremoni end captain resteth medina
two day end pilgrim may finish deuotion
ceremoni depart iambor A good day iourney thenc
steep mountain ouer passag sau one narrow path
call demir capi time past call yron gate Of
gate mahumetan say alli companion sonn law
mahumet pursu mani christian com vnto
mountain see way wherebi flee drew sword
strike said mountain diuid sunder pass thorow sau
life side moreouer alli among persian
greater reuerenc mahumet affirm sayd alli hath
done greater thing miracul mahumet therefor
esteem god almighti fellow but return matter
captain carouan within two day returneth cairo
com ezlem findeth captain threescor hors come
thither bring refresh said captain pilgrimag
also sell vnto pilgrim victual from thenc set forward
com birca within two leagu cairo master
hous bassha cairo horsemen come thither
receiu sumptuou costli banket made cost
basha captain retinu well refresh
departeth toward castl cairo salut basha receiu
great ioy gladness token good wil presenteth
garment cloth gold rich captain take alcaron
chest presenteth basha hau kiss
commandeth lay vp again some affirm
arriu cairo kill goodli camel cari alcaron
eat noth superstiti
contrari gain world would kill but
casual die case happi bless think
themselu get morsel eat and thu much concern
voyag captain carouan cairo

east india beyond indi wherein contein custom
rite countri merchandis commod well
gold siluer spice drugg pearl iewel
translat italian M thoma hickock

caesar frederick reader

sidenot caesar frederick trauell eighteen yeer east
indi hau gentl reader space eighteen yeer
continu coast trauell east indi
mani countrey beyond indi wherein haue good
ill success trauel hau seen vnderstood mani thing
woorthi note knowen world neuer
yet written thought good see almighti giuen
grace long peril pass long voyag return
mine own countrey nobl citi venic say thought good
briefli could write set forth voyag made
maruel thing haue seen trauel indi the mighti
princ gouern countrey religion faith
haue rite custom vse liue diuer
success happen vnto mani countrey
abound spice drug iewel giu also profit
aduertis haue desir make voyag and
whole world may commodi reioyc
trauell haue caus print order present
vnto gentl lou reader varieti thing
heerein content hope shall great delight receiu and
thu god goodness keep


A voyag east indi beyond indi c

sidenot the authour go venic cypru tripoli In
yere lord god caesar frederick venic
desir see east part world ship self shipp
call gradaig venic certain marchandis gouern M
iacomo vatica bound cypru ship went
arriu cypru left ship went lesser
tripoli soria stay afterward took iourney
alepo acquaint self marchant armenia
moor marchant consort go ormu
wee depart alepo two day iourney half came
citi call bir


Of citi call bir

bir small citi scars maner victual nere vnto
wall citi runneth riuer euphrat sidenot the river
euphrat In citi marchant diuid themselu compani
accord merchandis haue either buy
make boat carri good babylon down riuer
euphrat charg master marin conduct boat
voyag boat maner flat bottom yet strong
strong seru one voyag
they made accord sholdness riuer
riuer mani place full great stone greatli hinder
troubl goe down riuer these boat seru one
voyag down riuer vnto villag call feluchia
imposs bring vp riuer back again sidenot feluchia
small citi euphrat At feluchia marchant pluck boat
piec els sell small price bir cost
marchant forti fifti chicken piec sell feluchia
seuen eight chicken piec marchant
return babylon back again haue marchandis good
oweth custom make return forti day thorow
wilderness pass way great deal lesser charg
way sidenot mosul and haue marchandis oweth
custom goe way mosul costeth great
charg carouan compani from bir marchant imbark
themselu feluchia ouer again babylon riuer haue good store
water shall make voyag fifteen eighteen day down
riuer water low hath rain
much troubl forti fifti day journey down
bark strike stone riuer
must vnlade great troubl lade again
haue mend therefor necessari neither doe
marchant go one boat alon two three one boat
split lost strike shold may haue anoth readi
take good vntil time haue mend broken
boat draw broken boat land mend hard
defend night great multitud arabian come
down robb sidenot the arabian theeue number like
ant riuer eueri night make fast boat
banckesid must keep good watch arabian
theeue number like ant yet come robb
kill steal run away harquebuz good weapon
stand greatli fear shot and pass
riuer euphrat bir feluchia certein place
must pass pay custom certain medin vpon bale
custom belong sonn aboris king arabian
desert hath certain citi villag riuer
euphrat


feluchia babylon

sidenot the old babylon hath great trade marchant still
feluchia villag come bir doe vnbark themselu
vnlade good distant babylon day iourney
half land babylon great citi popul
great trade stranger great thorowfar persia
turkia arabia often time goe thenc carouan
diuer countrey citi copiou victual
comm armenia down riuer tygri certain zattar
raff made blowen hide skinn call vtrij thi riuer tygri
doeth wash wall citi these raff bound fast togeth
lay board aforesayd blowen skinn board
lade commod come babylon vnlade
vnladen let wind skinn
lade cammel make anoth voyag thi citi babylon
situat kingdom persia gouern turk On
side riuer toward arabia ouer citi
fair place town fair bazarro marchant
mani lodg greatest part marchant stranger
come babylon lie marchand sidenot A bridg made
boat the pass ouer tygri babylon borough long
bridg made boat chain togeth great chain prouid
riuer waxeth great abund rain falleth
open bridg middl one half bridg
falleth wall babylon brink
borough side riuer long bridg open
pass riuer small boat great danger
smalness boat ouerlad
fierceness stream ouerthrowen el stream doth
cari away mean mani peopl lost drown
thing proof haue mani time seen

Of tower babylon

the tower nimrod babel situat side tygri arabia
great plain distant babylon seuen eight mile
tower ruinat eueri side fall
made great mountain hath form yet
great part stand compass almost couer
aforesayd fall tower build made four squar
brick brick made earth dri sunn maner
form follow first lay lay brick footnot these
brick thickn six seuen inch foot half squar
mat made cane squar brick stead lime
daub earth mat cane time strong
thing woonderful behold great antiqu haue
gone round haue found place hath bene
door entranc may iudgement circuit mile
rather less

thi tower effect contrari thing seen afar
seem small nere man commeth
bigger tower afar seemeth great thing
nerer come lesser My iudgment reason
tower set great plain hath noth
make shew sau ruin hath made round
respect descri farr piec
tower yet standeth mountain made substanc
hath fallen maketh greater shew shall find
com neer


babylon basora

from babylon depart basora ship self one bark
vse go riuer tigri babylon basora basora
babylon bark made maner fust galliot
speron couer poop haue pump
great abund pitch haue pitch
pitch haue abund two day iourney babylon nere vnto
riuer euphrat citi call heit nere vnto citi
great plain full pitch maruel behold thing almost
incred hole footnot thi hole commeth
pitch true water pitch runneth valley
iland pitch resteth water runneth riuer
euphrat maketh riuer brackish
smell pitch brimston earth continu throweth
pitch air continual smoak pitch throwen
forc hot falleth like sprinckl ouer
plain abund plain alway full pitch
more arabian place say hole mouth hell
trueth thing notabl mark pitch
whole peopl haue great benefit pitch bark bark
call daneck saffin when riuer tygri well replenish
water may pass babylon basora eight nine day
sometim sometim less half much
dai water low may sail day night
place way pay mani medin bail
water low day iourney


basora

sidenot zizarij ancient peopl basora citi arabian
old time gouern arabian call zizarij
gouern great turk keepeth armi great
charg

the arabian call zizarij haue possess great countrey
ouercom turk sea hath deuid
countrey iland channel eb flow sea
caus turk bring armi neither
sea land anoth reason inhabit iland
strong warlik men sidenot At castl corna riuer
euphrat tygri meet A day iourney come basora
shall haue littl castl fort set point
land riuer euphrat tygri meet togeth castl
call corna point two riuer make monstrou great
riuer runneth sea call gulf persia
toward south basora distant sea fifteen mile
citi great trade spice drugg come
ormu also great store corn rice date
countrey doth yeeld sidenot ormu barrenest iland
world ship self basora go ormu sail
thorow persian sea six hundr mile distanc basora
ormu sail small ship made board bound togeth
small cord rope stead calk lay between eueri board
certain straw haue sow board board togeth
straw between wherethorow commeth much water
danger sidenot carichij iland gulf persia
depart basora pass mile sea right hand
along gulf vntil length arriu iland call carichij
fro whenc sail ormu sight persian shore left
side right side toward arabia discouer infinit iland


ormu

ormu footnot ormu alway replenish abund victual

goa diu cambaia

goa principal citi portug haue indi
resid viceroy court minist king portugal
from ormu goa nine hundr four score ten mile distanc

daman basan tana

Of citi chaul palmer tree

beyond iland shall find chaul firm land two
citi one portug moor citi
portug haue situat lower gouerneth mouth
harbour strongli wall mile
half distant citi moor gouern king
zamalluco In time warr great ship come
citi moor portug ordin sinck
must perforc pass castl portug
citi port sea great citi haue vnto
great traffiqu trade merchandis sort spice
drugg silk cloth silk sandol marsin versin porcelan
china veluet scarlet come portugal meca
mani sort merchandis there come eueri yeer cochin
cananor tenn fifteen great shipp laden great nut cure
sugar made self nut call giagra tree whereon
nut doe grow call palmer tree thorowout
indi especi place goa great abund
like date tree In whole world
tree profit goodness tree neither doe
men reap much benefit tree doe
part serueth vse none woorthi
burnt with timber tree make shipp without
mixtur tree leaue thereof make sail
fruit thereof kind nut make wine
wine make sugar placetto wine gather
spring yeer middl tree continu
goeth runneth white liquour like vnto water time
yeer put vessel vnder eueri tree eueri euen morn
take away full distil fire maketh
strong liquour put but quantiti zibibbo
white black short time made perfect wine after
make nut great store oil tree make great
quantiti boord quarter build Of bark tree
make cabl rope furnitur shipp say
rope better made hemp they make
bow bedst indi fashion scauasch merchandis
the leaue cut small weaue make sail
maner ship el fine mat and first rind
nut stamp make thereof perfect ockam calk shipp
great small hard bark thereof make spoon
vessel meat wise part thereof throwen away
cast fire when mat green full
excel sweet water drink man thirsti liquour
one mat may satisfi himself nut ripeneth
liquour thereof turneth kernel there goeth chaul
mallaca indi macao portugal coast
melind ormu infinit number quantiti good

eueri sort great store boraso past great store fetida great

goa

sidenot the chief place portug indi goa
principal citi portug haue indi wherein viceroy

circuit fiue twenti thirti mile citi borough
reason bigg citi indi reason fair
iland farr fairer full goodli

goa encamp neer vnto riuer side armi two

bezeneg

the citi bezeneg sack yeer four king
moor great power might name four king
follow first call dialcan second zamaluc
third cotamaluc fourth viridi yet four king
abl ouercom citi king bezeneg treason the
king bezeneg gentil amongst
captain two notabl moor two
captain either charg threescor ten fourescor
thousand men these two captain one religion four
king moor wrought mean betray own king
hand footnot A vnkind wick treason
princ haue giu credit stranger rather
own natiu peopl the king bezeneg esteem forc
four king enemi went citi wage battel
field armi ioyn battel last
space four hour two traitour captain
chiefest fight compani turn face
king made disord armi astoni
set themselu flight thirti yeer kingdom gouern
three brethren tyrant keep right king
prison vse eueri yeer shew peopl
pleasur rule list these brethren three
captain belong father king kept prison
die left sonn yong took gouernment
themselu the chiefest three call ramaragio sate
royal throne call king second call
temiragio took gouernment third call
bengatr captain general armi these three brethren
battel chiefest last neuer
heard quick dead sidenot the sack citi one
temiragio fled battel hau lost one eye new
came citi ouerthrow battel wiue children
three tyrant lawful king kept prison fled away
spoil four king moor entr citi
bezeneg great triumph remain six moneth
search vnder hous place money thing
hidden depart own kingdom
abl maintain kingdom farr distant
own countrey

when king depart bezeneg temiragio return
citi begann repopul sent word goa
merchant hors bring would pay
well caus foresayd two merchant went
compani withal carri hors bezeneg
sidenot An excel good polici intrap men also tyrant made
order law merchant hors
taken foresayd battel warr although own
mark would giue much would besid

mean saw great store hors brought thither vnto
hee gaue merchant fair word vntill time saw
could bring then licenc merchant depart without
giu thing hors poor men saw
desper mad sorrow grief

discharg business necessari rest vntill
way cleer theeue time rang vp down and

own followeth present

mean hope escap iudgement come As soul

that bodi made again reason

business
